# Nuxeo Training - Document types
###What we want to do ####At the end of the course: - A custom document type: Book - Use common metadata - Title - Contains custom metadatas - ISBN (string) - Author (String) - publicationDate (date) - rating (int) - Won't display/edit the metadata yet ! - Create Book document in Nuxeo
## What’s a Document?
## Not a file !

### Document type ? Defined by: - a unique name File, Note or Book - an optional super Document Type  - a set of schemas  - Define storage structure  - a set of facets - Define document behavior or capabilities - Folderish, Versionable, Commentable
### Document type in Studio ![New Document type in Studio](img/doctype-studio-newtype.png)
### Document type definition in Studio ![Document type definition in Studio](img/doctype-studio-definition.png)
### Document type definition ####Additional properties - Labels - Category
Where the document will be display at creation time
- Icons - Container types
Where the document type can be created
### Schemas - Defined by: - a unique name - a prefix (a kind of namespace or short name) - Storage part, define the metadata storage structure - A set of different fields/metadatas  - Each metadata has: - A name  - A type 
###Schema metadata types - Common metadata types are: - string - int - float - date - blob (complex) - complex - Complex type: a composite field of several fields - for instance an address complex type would look like: - street_number (string) - street (string) - zip code (string) - city (string) - country (string) - Each field can be multivalued

- Default schemas already imported - Add the schemas to use in your document type
### Schema tab in Document Type section Reusable only for the document type ![Schema tab](img/doctype-studio-schema2.png)
### Schemas are reusable - reusable by several doc types - Studio created schema for a doc type technically reusable
The schema created and available in the schema of the document type can't be reuse un studio, but actually can be reuse using Nuxeo extension point
- from Nuxeo: - dublincore - common - uid - file - files
###dublincore schema - Defined in almost all document types - Prefix: dc #### Metadatas: - Title title
Most important metadata of the document: Label of the document everywhere in the UI
- Description description - Nature nature
Nature of the document.
- Subjects subjects
Topic(s) of the document.
- Coverage
Information about the geographic reach of the document.
- Created at
Date automatically filled in by the system when the document is created.
- Last modified at
Date automatically filled in by the system when the document is modified.
- Author
User who created the document. This field is automatically filled in by the system.
- Contributors
Users who modified the document. This field is automatically filled in by the system.
- Last contributor
Last user who modified the document. This field is automatically filled in by the system.
####Access to a property of the document - dc:title - dc:nature - etc ...
###Facets - Added to a document or a document type - Tell the framework : «this document can support such behavior» - Can come with schemas - Folderish, Commentable, Versionable, Publishable, ... - Example: The tab Publishing appears only with the facet Publishable - Facets are inherited
when a document type inherits from another one
# Exercise - Document types
### Exercise - Document types - Book library (1/2) ####In Nuxeo Studio - Define a new book schema, containing the following fields - Let’s say that, for now, a Book is defined by:  - Its ISBN isbn (string)  - Its author (string)  - Its publication date publicationDate (date)  - A rating (int) - Define a new Book document type. Keep the default settings but - Extends: Document - the label: Book - the icons: files/book.png / files/book_100.png [github.com/nuxeo/nuxeo-sample-project](http://github.com/nuxeo/nuxeo-sample-project) - the category: Document - the additional schemas: book
### Exercise - Document types - Book library (2/2) #### Try out your changes - Start your Nuxeo DM server  - In Nuxeo DM, go to the Admin Center  - Connect to the admin center  - If not done, - register your instance of Nuxeo DM with your connect account (Admin Center → Nuxeo Connect) - set your instance in Dev Mode (Admin Center → Update center → nuxeo studio → dev mode)
Dev mode activated, you won't need to reboot the server for each changes
- Synchronize your Nuxeo Studio configuration with Nuxeo DM (Admin Center → Update center → nuxeo studio → update)  - Create new Book documents in Nuxeo #### Facets - The Edit tab don't contain the versioning options. The History tab don't contain the Archived versions tab - In studio, set the Versionable facet to your Book type and update Nuxeo Server - The versioning options and the Archived versions tab should appear The field we have setted are not display nor editable yet. We'll do it in the next section.
## Thank you!
